#define .4 .47				.3 .35

# standard actions ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
GUI_ACTION
	NAME GetHotAction
	# $param0 is the help text
	# $param1 set to non-zero to play the hotsound
	GUI_COMMAND SetHelpText $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN $param1 0 PlayHotSound END
END
	
GUI_ACTION
	NAME PlayNothing

END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME PlayHotSound

END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME PlaySelect

	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_BOND_SOUND buttons/fe.wav 1.0 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME ChangeButtonFocus
	# $param0 == string name of button to change focus to

	GUI_COMMAND PlaySelect END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_FOCUS $param0 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME STD_BUTTON_ACTION
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 ChangeButtonFocus THIS_GENERIC END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_FOCUS THIS_GENERIC END
END
 

# variables required for the text window element
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME TextWindowDataSourceCommandInput
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 9999
END
GUI_VARIABLE_STRING
	NAME TextWindowDataSourceCommandIsOutputValid
	VALUE "false"
END
GUI_VARIABLE_STRING
	NAME TextWindowDataSourceCommandOutputData
	VALUE " "
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME DoLoadGame
	# $param0 contains the launchstring
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE SETCVAR sv_newunit 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE "maxplayers 1" END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE $param0 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME DoConnectToServer
	# $param0 is the string var of the server to connect to
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE SETCVAR sv_newunit 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADD "connect " END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE $param0 QUOTED END
END


# checkbox and radio button stuff -----------------------------------------------------------------	
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 

GUI_ACTION
	NAME SetCheck
	# $param0 is the variable to change
	# $param1 is the new value
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE $param0 $param1 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME ToggleCheck
	# $param0 is the variable to toggle
	
	# oy, make a copy to test against
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE TEMP_VAR $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE $param0 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE $param0 1 END
END

GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME CB_STATE
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 5
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME UpdateCheckState
	# $param0 is the check variable
	
	# compute the new element state
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE CB_STATE 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE CB_STATE 3 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS CURRENT_ELEMENT_STATE 2 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE CB_STATE 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS CURRENT_ELEMENT_STATE 3 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE CB_STATE 2 END
END

 
 
 
 

 
 

 
 
 
 
 
 

	
# slider bar stuff -----------------------------------------------------------------	
 
 
 
 

GUI_ACTION
	NAME SliderUpdate	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SLIDER_HELPER UPDATE 12 $param0 $param1 $param2 $param3 $param4 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME SliderRefresh	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SLIDER_HELPER REFRESH 12 $param0 $param1 $param2 $param3 END
END

 

 
	
# edit box stuff ---------------------------------------------------------------------
 
 
 

 
 
 

GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME EDIT_STATE
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 3
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME UpdateEditState
	# $param0 is the string holding the results
	
	# compute the new element state
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE EDIT_STATE 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS CURRENT_ELEMENT_STATE 3 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE EDIT_STATE 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS CURRENT_ELEMENT_STATE 2 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE EDIT_STATE 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS CURRENT_ELEMENT_STATE 4 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE EDIT_STATE 2 END

	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE TEMP_VAR 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER ISEDITING $param0 TEMP_VAR END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE EDIT_STATE 3 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME TempEditSetParams
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER SETPARAMS $param0 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME EditBoxInputCancel
	# $param0 is the string variable
	# $param1 is a no-param action to call if not editing
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER ISEDITING $param0 TEMP_VAR END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 1 GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER ENDENTRY 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 0 $param1 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME EditBoxInputAccept
	# $param0 is the string variable
	# $param1 is the control
	# $param2 is an action that sets up the editing parameters

	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER ISEDITING $param0 TEMP_VAR END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 0 BeginTextEntry $param0 $param1 $param2 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 1 GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER ENDENTRY 1 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME BeginTextEntry
	# $param0 is the string variable
	# $param1 is the control
	# $param2 is an action that sets up the editing parameters
	
	# first stop our current selection
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER ISEDITING ANY TEMP_VAR END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 1 GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER ENDENTRY 1 END
	
	# start editing the new one
	GUI_COMMAND $param2 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER BEGINENTRY $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_FOCUS $param1 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME EndTextEntry

	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER ISEDITING $param0 TEMP_VAR END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 1 GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER ENDENTRY $param1 END
END

 
 

 


# tab-style buttons ---------------------------------------------------------------------
 
 
 
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME TAB_STATE
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 5
END
# norm,
# press,
# hot,
# current,norm
# current,press
# current,hot
GUI_ACTION
	NAME UpdateTabBtnState
	# $param0 is 1 if current, 0 if not
	# $param1 is the element state
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE TAB_STATE 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param1 2 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE TAB_STATE 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param1 3 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE TAB_STATE 2 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE TAB_STATE 3 END
END

# chicks! ------------------------------------------------------------
GUI_VARIABLE_MOVIE
	NAME dancin_chick_pic
#	TEXTURE "movies/i_bondgirl_4.avi"
	LOOPING FALSE
	AUDIO FALSE
END

GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME chicknum
	INITIAL_VALUE 0.01
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 1
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME chickpos
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 1
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME PickNewChick
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_MOVIE_VARIABLE dancin_chick_pic STOP END
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE chicknum RANDOMINT END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE chickpos RANDOM END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS chicknum 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE dancin_chick_pic "movies/girl_01.avi" 
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS chicknum 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE dancin_chick_pic "movies/girl_02.avi" 

	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_MOVIE_VARIABLE dancin_chick_pic PLAY END
END

 

# Top menu bar layout -----------------------------------------------------------------	
 
 
 
 
 
 

 
 
 

 

 
GUI_ACTION 
	NAME DoMoveHighlight
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE current_selected_top_button $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE dest_top_button $param0 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE tab_show_0 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS $param0 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE tab_show_0 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE tab_show_1 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE tab_show_1 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 2 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE tab_show_2 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS $param0 2 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE tab_show_2 0 END
END
GUI_ACTION 
	NAME TryMoveHighlight
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN current_selected_top_button dest_top_button GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE current_selected_top_button -0.1 END
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN current_selected_top_button dest_top_button GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE current_selected_top_button 0.1 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND UpdateTab0 END
	GUI_COMMAND UpdateTab1 END
	GUI_COMMAND UpdateTab2 END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE current_selected_top_button dest_top_button END
END

# the top button highlight thingy
GUI_ACTION 
	NAME ChooseNewButton
	GUI_COMMAND DoMoveHighlight $param0
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE dest_top_button $param0
	GUI_COMMAND ChangeButtonFocus $param1 END
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME current_selected_top_button
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 2
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME dest_top_button
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 2
END

# screen 0 update funcs and variables --------------
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME tab_show_0
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 1
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME ShowTab0
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN current_selected_top_button 1 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE tab_show_0 0.1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS current_selected_top_button 1 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE tab_show_0 0.1 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME HideTab0
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN tab_show_0 0 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE tab_show_0 -0.1 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME UpdateTab0
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS dest_top_button 0 ShowTab0 END 
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS dest_top_button 0 HideTab0 END 
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME TryFadeHiliteOut
	# $param0 is the state
	
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN $param0 0 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE $param0 -3 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME TryFadeHiliteIn
	# $param0 is the state
	
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS $param0 100 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE $param0 100 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME UpdateHiliteState
	# $param0 is the visibility
	# $param1 is the state
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 0 TryFadeHiliteOut $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 TryFadeHiliteIn $param1 END
END

 
 
 
 
 
 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

GUI_ACTION
	NAME SetDomePic
	# $param0 ... 1 to turn on, 0 to turn off
	# $param1 ... the texture, only valid if $param0 is 1
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE dome_pic_vis $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE dome_pic_tex $param1 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME SetDomePicVar
	# $param0 ... 1 to turn on, 0 to turn off
	# $param1 ... the texture, only valid if $param0 is 1
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE dome_pic_vis $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE dome_pic_tex $param1 END
END

	NAME mm_can_exit
	INITIAL_VALUE 0.0
	MIN_VALUE 0.0
	MAX_VALUE 1.0
END 

GUI_ACTION
	NAME MainMenuClose
	
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_FILE_PARSER CLOSE END
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE SAVE "nightfire"" END
	GUI_COMMAND GameSpySettingsSaveFunc END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE CLOSE END
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_MUSIC STOP ambient END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE WRITECONFIG END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME ExitMainMenu
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mm_can_exit 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS mm_can_exit 0.0 ChangeButtonFocus btn_main_singleplayer END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS mm_can_exit 0.0 GUI_ACTION_EXIT END
END

	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_DIALOG LOADACTION GUI_SETTINGS_FILE END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_DIALOG LOADACTION GUI_ACTION_BOT_HELPER END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_DIALOG LOADACTION GUI_FILE_PARSER END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_DIALOG LOADACTION GUI_ACTION_MUSIC END
	
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_FILE_PARSER OPEN "gui/Scripts/Mainmenu/creditslist.txt" END	
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE LOAD "nightfire"" END
	GUI_COMMAND GameSpySettingsLoadFunc END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE CLOSE END
	
	GUI_COMMAND MultiplayerInitialize END	
	GUI_COMMAND OptionsInitialize END	
		
	GUI_COMMAND CountSaveGames END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE nightfire_initialized 1 END
		
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS console 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mm_can_exit 1 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_MUSIC PLAY gui ambient frontend_ectest.ogg 0 100 5000 5000 END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_MUSIC PLAY gui ambient frontend_full.ogg 0 100 5000 0000 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME MainFrameFunc
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS nightfire_initialized 0 InitNightfire END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS getsaveCount 0 CountSaveGames END
END


# fading in and out --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 
 

GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME mainFadeinTimer
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 21
	WRAP FALSE
	LOOP FALSE
	RUNNING FALSE
	LERP_TIME 21
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME mainFadeDir
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE -1
	MAX_VALUE 1
END

# 0 for "map" 1 for "changelevel"
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME MPStartGameType
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 1
END

 

GUI_ACTION
	NAME CheckFadeIn
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN mainFadeinTimer 2 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mainFadeDir 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS mainFadeinTimer 2 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mainFadeDir 0 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS mainFadeDir 0 GUI_ACTION_VCR_VARIABLE mainFadeinTimer PAUSE END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS mainFadeDir 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mainFadeinTimer 2 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME CheckFadeOut
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN mainFadeinTimer 4 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mainFadeDir 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN mainFadeinTimer 4 GUI_ACTION_VCR_VARIABLE mainFadeinTimer PAUSE END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN mainFadeinTimer 4 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mainFadeinTimer 0 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME CheckFade
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS mainFadeDir -1 CheckFadeOut END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS mainFadeDir 1 CheckFadeIn END
END

	NAME ActivateMainMenu
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mainFadeDir 1 END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_VCR_VARIABLE mainFadeinTimer REWIND END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_VCR_VARIABLE mainFadeinTimer PLAY END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param1 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_FOCUS $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param1 1 ChangeButtonFocus $param0 END
END

	NAME ExitMissionSelect
	
	GUI_COMMAND ChangeButtonFocus btn_sp_mission_select END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME ActivateMissionSelect
	
	GUI_COMMAND SetScreenTitle "MISSION SELECT" END
	GUI_COMMAND ChangeButtonFocus btn_ms_back END
	GUI_COMMAND MissionSetPic END
	GUI_COMMAND MissionSetText END
END

	NAME GetCharacterModel

GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME model_dm	# a cvar
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 25
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME model_mi6	# a cvar
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 9
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME model_phx	# a cvar
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 16
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME Editagent_Initialize
	
	GUI_COMMAND SetDMCharacterVar model_dm END
	GUI_COMMAND SetTP_MI6_CharacterVar model_mi6 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE TEMP_VAR model_phx END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE TEMP_VAR 10 END
	GUI_COMMAND SetTP_phoenix_CharacterVar TEMP_VAR END
	
	
	GUI_COMMAND InitConnectSpeed END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE editagent_dmname cl_name END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME Editagent_ApplyChoices

	GUI_COMMAND ApplyConnectSpeed END
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE cl_name editagent_dmname END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADD "cl_name " END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE editagent_dmname END
	
	# deathmatch prefs
	
	# apply the dm model number
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADD "model_dm " END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE ea_model_dm_index END
	
	# teamplay prefs
	
	# apply the team mi6 model name
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADD "model_mi6 " END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE ea_model_tp_mi6_index END
	
	# apply the team phoenix model name
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE TEMP_VAR ea_model_tp_phx_index END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE TEMP_VAR -10 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADD "model_phx " END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE TEMP_VAR END
END

# options --------------------------------------------------------------------
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME mp_hq_models	#a cvar
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 1
END
GUI_VARIABLE_STRING
	NAME ea_mp_decals
	VALUE "1000"
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME SetEditDecalsParams
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER SETPARAMS STYLE "NUMERIC" END	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER SETPARAMS LENGTH 6 END	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER SETPARAMS NUMRANGE 0 999999 END	
END

# connection speed (rate)
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME rate	# also a cvar!
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 99999
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME ea_opt_speed
	INITIAL_VALUE 1
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 2
	WRAP TRUE
END
GUI_VARIABLE_STRING
	NAME ea_opt_speed_text
	VALUE " "
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME ea_speed_changed
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 1
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME InitConnectSpeed
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_opt_speed 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_speed_changed 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN rate 3000 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_opt_speed 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN rate 5000 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_opt_speed 2 END
	GUI_COMMAND GetConnectSpeedText END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME _ApplyConnectSpeed
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS ea_opt_speed 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE rate 3000 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS ea_opt_speed 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE rate 5000 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS ea_opt_speed 2 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE rate 10000 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME ApplyConnectSpeed
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS ea_speed_changed 1 _ApplyConnectSpeed END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_speed_changed 0 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME GetConnectSpeedText
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS ea_opt_speed 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_opt_speed_text "56K" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS ea_opt_speed 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_opt_speed_text "ISDN" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS ea_opt_speed 2 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_opt_speed_text "CABLE/DSL/T1" END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME ChooseNextConnectSpeed

	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE ea_opt_speed 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 -1 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE ea_opt_speed -1 END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS $param0 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_speed_changed 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND GetConnectSpeedText END
END

# hot stuff -----------------------------------------------------------------
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME ea_dm_hot
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 1
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME ea_tp_hot
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 1
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME EASetHotMode
	# $param0 is 0 for none, 1 for dm and 2 for tp
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_dm_hot 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_tp_hot 0 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_dm_hot 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 SetHelpText "Choose the character you would like to play in Combat Training games." END
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 2 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_tp_hot 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 2 SetHelpText "Choose the characters you would like to play when on Team MI6 and Team Phoenix in teamplay games." END
END

	NAME SetDMCharacter
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE ea_model_dm_index $param0 END

	GUI_COMMAND GetDMCharacterPic ea_model_dm_index ea_dm_chartex END
END

	GUI_COMMAND GetDMCharacterPic ea_model_dm_index ea_dm_chartex END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME StartNewServer
	
	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND Create_ApplyBots END	
	
	# server name
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE SETCVAR "host_name" create_servername END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADD "host_name " END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE create_servername QUOTED END
	
	# password
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE SETCVAR "sv_password" create_password END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADD "sv_password " END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE create_password QUOTED END
	
	# maxplayers
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADD "maxplayers " END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE create_maxplayers END
	
	# add gametype
	GUI_COMMAND AddGametype END
	
	# add game options
	GUI_COMMAND AddGameOptions END
	
	# set public/lan mode
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE SETCVAR "sv_lan" create_lan END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADD "sv_lan " END
#	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE create_lan END
	
	# start the map
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_MAP_HELPER GETMAPFILE create_map_index map_filename END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS MPStartGameType 0 GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADD "map " END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS MPStartGameType 1 GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADD "changelevel " END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_EXECUTE ADDLINE map_filename END
		
	# close the menu
	GUI_COMMAND ExitMainMenu 1 END
END

END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME SetMapListType
	# $param0 is 0 for dm, 1 for tdm or 2 for ctf
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 0 GUI_ACTION_MAP_HELPER SETCURRENTTYPE "DM" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_MAP_HELPER SETCURRENTTYPE "TDM" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 2 GUI_ACTION_MAP_HELPER SETCURRENTTYPE "CTF" END
	
	GUI_COMMAND SetMapListIndex 0 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME UpdateCreateBotsVisibility
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE create_bots_visible 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS create_bots 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE create_bots_visible 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS create_fillbots 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE create_bots_visible 0 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS create_bots_visible 1 UpdateBotList END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_BOT_HELPER ENABLEBOTS create_bots_visible END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME UpdateBotList
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_BOT_HELPER GETPARAMS "bot" create_botslist_top 7 END
END

	NAME BotFrameUpdate

	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 1 UpdateBotList END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS create_addbot_valid 1 GUI_ACTION_BOT_HELPER ADDBOT create_addbot_skin create_addbot_name create_addbot_skill END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS create_addbot_valid 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE create_addbot_valid 0 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME ClickStopUpdate
	
	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY STOPUPDATELIST END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME ClickSetGameSpyMode
	
	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND SetGameSpyMode $param0
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME SetGameSpyMode
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY STOPUPDATELIST CLEARLIST END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 0 GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SETMODE INTERNET END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SETMODE LAN END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE gspy_mode $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND HandleGameSpyChange END
	GUI_COMMAND SetGamespyDomePic END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME SetGamespyDomePic
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_mode 0 SetDomePic 1 "gui/frontend/i_multiplayer_internet.png" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_mode 1 SetDomePic 1 "gui/frontend/i_multiplayer_lan.png" END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME GameSpyInit	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_initialized 0 GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY INITIALIZE END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_initialized 0 SetGameSpyMode 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_initialized 0 GameSpyFrameFunc END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_initialized 0 SetTopServer 0 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SETSORTPRI 3 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SETSORTPRI 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SETSORTPRI 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND RefreshSortPriorities END
	GUI_COMMAND ApplyAllFilters END
	
	GUI_COMMAND GetPingFilterStr END
	GUI_COMMAND GetGameFilterStr END
	
	GUI_COMMAND SetGamespyDomePic END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE gspy_initialized 1 END
	
	# load our settings here
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME GameSpySettingsLoadFunc

	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE VARIABLE join_filter_ping END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE VARIABLE join_filter_game END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE VARIABLE join_filter_nopassword END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE VARIABLE join_filter_nolisten END	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY LOADFAVORITES END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME GameSpySettingsSaveFunc

	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE VARIABLE join_filter_ping END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE VARIABLE join_filter_game END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE VARIABLE join_filter_nopassword END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_SETTINGS_FILE VARIABLE join_filter_nolisten END	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SAVEFAVORITES END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME GameSpyShutdown	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE gspy_initialized 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SHUTDOWN END
	GUI_COMMAND UpdateServerListView END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME HandleGameSpyChange
	
	GUI_COMMAND UpdateServerListView END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD SELECTEDINDEX gspy_selected_server gspy_top_server END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME GameSpyFrameFunc
	
	# get the server count
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD SERVERCOUNT gspy_total_servers END
	
	# update the listing status
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD SL_STATUS gspy_status_num END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE gspy_status_text " " END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE gspy_refresh_pct 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_status_num 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE gspy_status_text "Idle" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_status_num 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE gspy_status_text "Getting List" END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN gspy_status_num 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE gspy_status_text "Refreshing Servers" END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN gspy_status_num 99 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE gspy_refresh_pct gspy_status_num END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN gspy_refresh_pct 99 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE gspy_refresh_pct -100 END
	
	# if the list was invalidated in our view, refresh it
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY INVALIDATED gspy_top_server 17 TEMP_VAR END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 1 HandleGameSpyChange END
END

GUI_VARIABLE_STRING
	NAME gspy_con_str
	VALUE "  "
END	

GUI_ACTION
	NAME OpenPasswordDialog
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_DIALOG OPENMENU "gui/Scripts/Dialogs/dlg_password.txt" END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_DIALOG SETVARIABLE "gui/Scripts/Dialogs/dlg_password.txt" join_address gspy_con_str END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME FinishConnect
	
	# connect!
	GUI_COMMAND DoConnectToServer gspy_con_str END
	
	# close the menu	
	GUI_COMMAND ExitMainMenu 1 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME ConnectToServer
	
	# get the connect address
	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND SetWorkingGamespyServer gspy_selected_server END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD CONNECTSTRING gspy_con_str END
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD "password" TEMP_VAR END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 1 OpenPasswordDialog END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS TEMP_VAR 0 FinishConnect END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME ClickOnServerSlot
	# $param0 is the index you clicked on
	
	GUI_COMMAND SetWorkingGamespyServer $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SELECTSERVER END	# selects the current working server
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD SELECTEDINDEX gspy_selected_server gspy_top_server END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME ScrollTopServerIndex
	# $param0 is the number of items to scroll and the direction
	
	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE TEMP_VAR gspy_top_server END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SETSCROLL gspy_top_server $param0 17 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETSCROLLFRAC gspy_top_server join_scrollFrac 17 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS TEMP_VAR gspy_top_server HandleGameSpyChange END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME SetTopServer
	# param0 = 0-based index to set to top
	
	# this will compute the max index allowed into the list, based on total servers and servers per page
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE gspy_tmp gspy_total_servers END
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN gspy_tmp 17 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE gspy_tmp 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_tmp 17 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE gspy_tmp 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN gspy_tmp 17 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE gspy_tmp -SERVERS_PER_PAGE END
	
	# if we're higher than the max server index, clamp the value
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE gspy_top_server $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN gspy_top_server gspy_tmp GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE gspy_top_server gspy_tmp END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME SetWorkingGamespyServer
	# $param0 == index from top
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SETWORKINGSERVER gspy_top_server $param0 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME GetServerInfo
	# $param0 == index from top
	# $param1 == float variable to put the password
	# $param2 == float variable to put the server type (dedicated, etc.)
	# $param3 == float variable to put the favorite (0 through 3)	
	# $param4 == string variable to put the hostname
	# $param5 == float variable to put the ping
	# $param6 == string variable to put the mapname
	# $param7 == string variable to put the gametype
	# $param8 == string variable to put the players
	
	GUI_COMMAND SetWorkingGamespyServer $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD "password"		$param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD "dedicated" 	$param2 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD FAVORITE		$param3 END	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD "hostname"		$param4 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD SERVERPING		$param5 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD "mapname"		$param6 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD "gametype"		$param7 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD SERVERPLAYERS	$param8 END
END

	NAME UpdateLanTab
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_mode 1 UpdateTabBtnState 1 CURRENT_ELEMENT_STATE END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_mode 0 UpdateTabBtnState 0 CURRENT_ELEMENT_STATE END
END

	NAME UpdateInternetTab
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_mode 0 UpdateTabBtnState 1 CURRENT_ELEMENT_STATE END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS gspy_mode 1 UpdateTabBtnState 0 CURRENT_ELEMENT_STATE END
END

	NAME ChangeSortPriority
	# $param0 is the var to move to top priority

	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SETSORTPRI $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND RefreshSortPriorities END
END

GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME FAV_STATE
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 12
END		
GUI_ACTION
	NAME UpdateFavoritesState
	# $param0 is the state variable
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE FAV_STATE 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS CURRENT_ELEMENT_STATE 3 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE FAV_STATE 4 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS CURRENT_ELEMENT_STATE 2 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE FAV_STATE 8 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE FAV_STATE 1 END	# favorite
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 2 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE FAV_STATE 3 END	# dont like
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 3 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE FAV_STATE 2 END	# played
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 0 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE FAV_STATE 4 END	# dont care
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 -1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE FAV_STATE 0 END
END		

 

GUI_ACTION
	NAME FavoriteButtonClick
	# $param0 is the index
	# $param1 is the variable
	
	GUI_COMMAND SetWorkingGamespyServer $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY TOGGLEFAVORITE END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY GETFIELD FAVORITE $param1 END	
END

 
 
 
 
 
 
 


GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME PING_VAL
	INITIAL_VALUE -1
	MIN_VALUE -1
	MAX_VALUE 7
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME UpdatePingValue
	
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN $param0 400 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE PING_VAL 7 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 400 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE PING_VAL 6 END
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN $param0 400 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE PING_VAL 6 END
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN $param0 300 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE PING_VAL 5 END
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN $param0 200 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE PING_VAL 4 END
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN $param0 150 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE PING_VAL 3 END
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN $param0 100 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE PING_VAL 2 END
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN $param0 50 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE PING_VAL 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN $param0 25 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE PING_VAL 0 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 -1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE PING_VAL -1 END
END

 

# filtering stuff -----------------------------------------------------------
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME join_filter_ping
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 4
	WRAP TRUE
END
GUI_VARIABLE_STRING
	NAME join_filter_ping_str
	VALUE "  "
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME GetPingFilterStr
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS join_filter_ping 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE join_filter_ping_str "All" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS join_filter_ping 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE join_filter_ping_str "<50" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS join_filter_ping 2 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE join_filter_ping_str "<100" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS join_filter_ping 3 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE join_filter_ping_str "<200" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS join_filter_ping 4 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE join_filter_ping_str "<400" END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME CyclePingFilter
	
	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN $param0 0 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE join_filter_ping 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN $param0 0 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE join_filter_ping -1 END
	GUI_COMMAND GetPingFilterStr END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SETFILTER PING join_filter_ping END
END

GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME join_filter_game
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 3
	WRAP TRUE
END

	NAME join_filter_game_str
	VALUE "  "
END

	NAME GetGameFilterStr
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS join_filter_game 0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE join_filter_game_str "All" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS join_filter_game 1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE join_filter_game_str "CT" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS join_filter_game 2 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE join_filter_game_str "TEAM CT" END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS join_filter_game 3 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE join_filter_game_str "CTF" END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME CycleGameFilter
	
	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND GREATERTHAN $param0 0 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE join_filter_game 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND LESSTHAN $param0 0 GUI_ACTION_ADD_VARIABLE join_filter_game -1 END
	GUI_COMMAND GetGameFilterStr END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_GAMESPY SETFILTER GAME join_filter_game END
END

# contains primarily variables and actions for the key bind system

GUI_ACTION
	NAME ControlsLoadDefaults
	
	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND SetSensitivity 2 END
	GUI_COMMAND SetMouseInvert 0 END
		
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_KEY_CONFIG CLEARBINDINGS END	
	GUI_COMMAND LoadDefaultBindings END
	GUI_COMMAND UpdateBindings END
END

#mouse invert variable
GUI_ACTION
	NAME ControlsSetup
	
	GUI_COMMAND IntroduceKeyRepresentations END
	GUI_COMMAND IntroduceBindings END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_KEY_CONFIG LOADBINDINGS END	
	GUI_COMMAND SetControlBank1 END
	GUI_COMMAND RefreshControlSettings END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME RefreshControlSettings
	GUI_COMMAND UpdateBindings END
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS GETFIELD MOUSE_INVERT mouse_invertvar END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS GETFIELD MOUSE_SENSITIVITY mouse_sensitivity_value END
	GUI_COMMAND SliderRefresh 1 20 mouse_sensitivity_value mouse_sensitivity_frac END
	
	GUI_COMMAND ResetChangedBools END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME Controls_Apply
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS mInvertChanged 1 GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS SETFIELD MOUSE_INVERT mouse_invertvar END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS mSensitivityChanged 1 GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS SETFIELD MOUSE_SENSITIVITY mouse_sensitivity_value END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_KEY_CONFIG SAVEBINDINGS END	
		
	GUI_COMMAND ResetChangedBools END
END

GUI_ACTION 
	NAME ResetChangedBools
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mInvertChanged 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mSensitivityChanged 0 END
END

# mouse sensitivity variables and actions ---------------------------------------------------
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME mSensitivityChanged
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 1
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME mouse_sensitivity_value
	INITIAL_VALUE 1
	MIN_VALUE 1
	MAX_VALUE 20
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME mouse_sensitivity_frac
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 1
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME SetSensitivity
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mouse_sensitivity_value $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND SensitivitySliderRefresh END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mSensitivityChanged 1 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME SensitivitySliderRefresh
	GUI_COMMAND SliderRefresh 1 20 mouse_sensitivity_value mouse_sensitivity_frac END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME DoSensitivitySliderClick
	
	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND SliderUpdate 1 20 mouse_sensitivity_value mouse_sensitivity_frac mouse_sens_slider END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mSensitivityChanged 1 END
END

	NAME mInvertChanged
	INITIAL_VALUE 0

	MAX_VALUE 1

	NAME mouse_invertvar
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 1

	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE mInvertChanged 1 END

# key binding actions and variables ------------------------------------------------------------
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME binding_index
	INITIAL_VALUE -1
	MIN_VALUE -1
	MAX_VALUE 20
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME binding_key
	INITIAL_VALUE -1
	MIN_VALUE -1
	MAX_VALUE 99999
END
GUI_VARIABLE_FLOAT
	NAME bind_status
	INITIAL_VALUE 0
	MIN_VALUE 0
	MAX_VALUE 3
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME PlayBindInvalid
	
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME PlayBindValid
	
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME PlayBindCancel
	
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME BindFrameCheck
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_KEY_CONFIG BINDSTATUS bind_status END	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS bind_status 2 PlayBindInvalid END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS bind_status 3 EndBinding 1 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME BindButtonCancel
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS binding_key -1 ExitSettingsMenu 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS binding_key -1 EndBinding 0 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME TryBeginBind
	
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS $param2 -1 ChangeButtonFocus $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS $param2 -1 BeginBinding $param0 $param2 END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME BindButtonUse
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS binding_key -1 TryBeginBind $param0 $param1 $param2 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME ChooseControlBank
	
	GUI_COMMAND STD_BUTTON_ACTION 1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 SetControlBank1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 2 SetControlBank2 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 3 SetControlBank3 END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME EndBinding
	
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_KEY_CONFIG ENDBIND END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE binding_key -1 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE binding_index -1 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 0 PlayBindCancel END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS $param0 1 PlayBindValid END
	GUI_COMMAND UpdateBindings END
END
GUI_ACTION
	NAME BeginBinding
	
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS $param1 -1 GUI_ACTION_KEY_CONFIG BEGINBIND $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS $param1 -1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE binding_key $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND NOTEQUALS $param1 -1 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE binding_index $param0 END
	GUI_COMMAND UpdateBindings END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME SetupBindSlot
	# $param0 is the slot
	# $param1 is the variable number to assign
	# $param2 is the literal string name
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 1 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot1 $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 2 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot2 $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 3 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot3 $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 4 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot4 $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 5 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot5 $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 6 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot6 $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 7 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot7 $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 8 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot8 $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 9 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot9 $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 10 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot10 $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 11 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot11 $param1 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 12 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE_VARIABLE kc_func_slot12 $param1 END
	
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 1 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE kc_funcname_slot1 $param2 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 2 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE kc_funcname_slot2 $param2 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 3 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE kc_funcname_slot3 $param2 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 4 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE kc_funcname_slot4 $param2 END

	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 6 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE kc_funcname_slot6 $param2 END

	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 8 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE kc_funcname_slot8 $param2 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 9 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE kc_funcname_slot9 $param2 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 10 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE kc_funcname_slot10 $param2 END

	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 12 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE kc_funcname_slot12 $param2 END

	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 2 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE kc_func_slot2 -1 END

	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS 4 $param0 GUI_ACTION_SET_VARIABLE kc_func_slot4 -1 END

	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS GETFIELD TEXTURE_QUALITY vid_hq_textures END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS GETFIELD TEXTURE_RESOLUTION vid_texture_res END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS GETFIELD MODEL_QUALITY vid_model_quality END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS GETFIELD EFFECTS_QUALITY vid_effects_quality END
	GUI_COMMAND RefreshBrightnessSlider END
	GUI_COMMAND Refresh_TexQualString END
	GUI_COMMAND Refresh_TexResString END
	GUI_COMMAND Refresh_ModelQualityString END
	GUI_COMMAND Refresh_EffectsQualityString END
END

	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS SETFIELD TEXTURE_QUALITY vid_hq_textures END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS SETFIELD TEXTURE_RESOLUTION vid_texture_res END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS SETFIELD MODEL_QUALITY vid_model_quality END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SERVER_OPTIONS SETFIELD EFFECTS_QUALITY vid_effects_quality END
END

	NAME SetEditVidDecalsParams
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_TEXT_ENTRY_HELPER SETPARAMS STYLE "NUMERIC" END

# ------------------------------------------------------------- screen definition -------------------------
GUI_ACTION
	NAME OptionsInitialize
	
	GUI_COMMAND ControlsSetup END
	GUI_COMMAND Video_Initialize END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME OptionsShutdown
	
	
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME ActivateSettingsMenu
	
	# reload the settings
	GUI_COMMAND RefreshControlSettings END
	GUI_COMMAND RefreshAudioSettings END
	
	# show the screen
	GUI_COMMAND SetScreenTitle OPTIONS END
	GUI_COMMAND DoMoveHighlight 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND GUI_ACTION_SET_FOCUS btn_set_controls END
END

GUI_ACTION
	NAME ExitSettingsMenu
	
	# save out the settings
	GUI_COMMAND Controls_Apply END
	GUI_COMMAND Video_Apply END
	
	# switch back to main menu
	GUI_COMMAND DoMoveHighlight 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND ActivateMainMenu btn_main_settings 1 END
END

# controls tab defines, variables and actions -------------------------

	NAME ControlsActivated
	
	GUI_COMMAND ChooseNewButton 0 btn_set_controls END
	GUI_COMMAND SetDomePic 0 END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS controls_control_bank 1 SetDomePic 1 gui/frontend/i_options_movement.png END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS controls_control_bank 2 SetDomePic 1 gui/frontend/i_options_actions.png END
	GUI_COMMAND EQUALS controls_control_bank 3 SetDomePic 1 gui/frontend/i_options_actions.png END
END

	NAME AudioActivated

END

END
